    71	 * isFalsy     : is falsy
    72	 * isJson      : is json
    73	 * isNumber    : is number
    74	 * isString    : is string
    75	 * isBoolean   : is boolean
    76	 * isArray     : is array
    77	 */
    78	const parseAssertionOperator = (str = '') => {
    79	  if (!str || typeof str !== 'string' || !str.length) {
    80	    return {
    81	      operator: 'eq',
    82	      value: str
    83	    };
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  const operators = [
    87	    'eq',
    88	    'neq',
    89	    'gt',
    90	    'gte',
    91	    'lt',
    92	    'lte',
    93	    'in',
    94	    'notIn',
    95	    'contains',
    96	    'notContains',
    97	    'length',
    98	    'matches',
    99	    'notMatches',
   100	    'startsWith',
   101	    'endsWith',
   102	    'between',
   103	    'isEmpty',
   104	    'isNotEmpty',
   105	    'isNull',
   106	    'isUndefined',
   107	    'isDefined',
   108	    'isTruthy',
   109	    'isFalsy',
   110	    'isJson',
   111	    'isNumber',
   112	    'isString',
   113	    'isBoolean',
   114	    'isArray'
   115	  ];
   116	
   117	  const unaryOperators = [
   118	    'isEmpty',
   119	    'isNotEmpty',
   120	    'isNull',
   121	    'isUndefined',
   122	    'isDefined',
   123	    'isTruthy',
   124	    'isFalsy',
   125	    'isJson',
   126	    'isNumber',
   127	    'isString',
   128	    'isBoolean',
   129	    'isArray'
   130	  ];
   131	
   132	  const [operator, ...rest] = str.trim().split(' ');
   133	  const value = rest.join(' ');
   134	
   135	  if (unaryOperators.includes(operator)) {
   136	    return {
   137	      operator,
   138	      value: ''
   139	    };
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  if (operators.includes(operator)) {
   143	    return {
   144	      operator,
   145	      value
   146	    };
   147	  }
   148	
   149	  return {
   150	    operator: 'eq',
   151	    value: str
   152	  };
   153	};
   154	
   155	const isUnaryOperator = (operator) => {
   156	  const unaryOperators = [
   157	    'isEmpty',
   158	    'isNotEmpty',
   159	    'isNull',
   160	    'isUndefined',
   161	    'isDefined',
   162	    'isTruthy',
   163	    'isFalsy',
   164	    'isJson',
   165	    'isNumber',
   166	    'isString',
   167	    'isBoolean',
   168	    'isArray'
   169	  ];
   170	
   171	  return unaryOperators.includes(operator);
   172	};
   173	
   174	const evaluateJsTemplateLiteralBasedOnRuntime = (literal, context, runtime) => {
   175	  if (runtime === 'quickjs') {
   176	    return executeQuickJsVm({
   177	      script: literal,
   178	      context,
   179	      scriptType: 'template-literal'
   180	    });
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  return evaluateJsTemplateLiteral(literal, context);
   184	};
   185	
   186	const evaluateJsExpressionBasedOnRuntime = (expr, context, runtime) => {
   187	  if (runtime === 'quickjs') {
   188	    return executeQuickJsVm({
   189	      script: expr,
   190	      context,
   191	      scriptType: 'expression'
   192	    });
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  return evaluateJsExpression(expr, context);
   196	};
   197	
   198	const evaluateRhsOperand = (rhsOperand, operator, context, runtime) => {
   199	  if (isUnaryOperator(operator)) {
   200	    return;
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  const interpolationContext = {
   204	    globalEnvironmentVariables: context.bru.globalEnvironmentVariables,
   205	    collectionVariables: context.bru.collectionVariables,
   206	    folderVariables: context.bru.folderVariables,
   207	    requestVariables: context.bru.requestVariables,
   208	    runtimeVariables: context.bru.runtimeVariables,
   209	    envVariables: context.bru.envVariables,
   210	    processEnvVars: context.bru.processEnvVars
   211	  };
   212	
   213	  // gracefully allow both a,b as well as [a, b]
   214	  if (operator === 'in' || operator === 'notIn') {
   215	    if (rhsOperand.startsWith('[') && rhsOperand.endsWith(']')) {
   216	      rhsOperand = rhsOperand.substring(1, rhsOperand.length - 1);
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    return rhsOperand
   220	      .split(',')
   221	      .map((v) =>
   222	        evaluateJsTemplateLiteralBasedOnRuntime(interpolateString(v.trim(), interpolationContext), context, runtime)
   223	      );
   224	  }
   225	
   226	  if (operator === 'between') {
   227	    const [lhs, rhs] = rhsOperand
   228	      .split(',')
   229	      .map((v) =>
   230	        evaluateJsTemplateLiteralBasedOnRuntime(interpolateString(v.trim(), interpolationContext), context, runtime)
   231	      );
   232	    return [lhs, rhs];
   233	  }
   234	
   235	  // gracefully allow both ^[a-Z] as well as /^[a-Z]/
   236	  if (operator === 'matches' || operator === 'notMatches') {
   237	    if (rhsOperand.startsWith('/') && rhsOperand.endsWith('/')) {
   238	      rhsOperand = rhsOperand.substring(1, rhsOperand.length - 1);
   239	    }
   240	
   241	    return interpolateString(rhsOperand, interpolationContext);
   242	  }
   243	
   244	  return evaluateJsTemplateLiteralBasedOnRuntime(interpolateString(rhsOperand, interpolationContext), context, runtime);
   245	};
   246	
   247	class AssertRuntime {
   248	  constructor(props) {
   249	    this.runtime = props?.runtime || 'quickjs';
   250	  }
   251	
   252	  runAssertions(assertions, request, response, envVariables, runtimeVariables, processEnvVars) {
   253	    const globalEnvironmentVariables = request?.globalEnvironmentVariables || {};
   254	    const oauth2CredentialVariables = request?.oauth2CredentialVariables || {};
   255	    const collectionVariables = request?.collectionVariables || {};
   256	    const folderVariables = request?.folderVariables || {};
   257	    const requestVariables = request?.requestVariables || {};
   258	    const enabledAssertions = _.filter(assertions, (a) => a.enabled);
   259	    if (!enabledAssertions.length) {
   260	      return [];
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    const promptVariables = request?.promptVariables || {};
   264	    const certsAndProxyConfig = request?.certsAndProxyConfig;
   265	    const bru = new Bru({
   266	      runtime: this.runtime,
   267	      envVariables,
   268	      runtimeVariables,
   269	      processEnvVars,
   270	      collectionVariables,
   271	      folderVariables,
   272	      requestVariables,
   273	      globalEnvironmentVariables,
   274	      promptVariables,
   275	      certsAndProxyConfig,
   276	      requestUrl: request?.url
   277	    });
   278	    const req = new BrunoRequest(request);
   279	    const res = createResponseParser(response);
   280	
   281	    const bruContext = {
   282	      bru,
   283	      req,
   284	      res
   285	    };
   286	
   287	    const context = {
   288	      ...globalEnvironmentVariables,
   289	      ...collectionVariables,
   290	      ...envVariables,
   291	      ...folderVariables,
   292	      ...requestVariables,
   293	      ...oauth2CredentialVariables,
   294	      ...runtimeVariables,
   295	      ...processEnvVars,
   296	      ...bruContext
   297	    };
   298	
   299	    const assertionResults = [];
   300	
   301	    // parse assertion operators
   302	    for (const v of enabledAssertions) {
   303	      const lhsExpr = v.name;
   304	      const rhsExpr = v.value;
   305	      const { operator, value: rhsOperand } = parseAssertionOperator(rhsExpr);
   306	
   307	      try {
   308	        const lhs = evaluateJsExpressionBasedOnRuntime(lhsExpr, context, this.runtime);
   309	        const rhs = evaluateRhsOperand(rhsOperand, operator, context, this.runtime);
   310	
   311	        switch (operator) {
   312	          case 'eq':
   313	            expect(lhs).to.equal(rhs);
   314	            break;
   315	          case 'neq':
   316	            expect(lhs).to.not.equal(rhs);
   317	            break;
   318	          case 'gt':
   319	            expect(lhs).to.be.greaterThan(rhs);
   320	            break;
   321	          case 'gte':
   322	            expect(lhs).to.be.greaterThanOrEqual(rhs);
   323	            break;
   324	          case 'lt':
   325	            expect(lhs).to.be.lessThan(rhs);
   326	            break;
   327	          case 'lte':
   328	            expect(lhs).to.be.lessThanOrEqual(rhs);
   329	            break;
   330	          case 'in':
   331	            expect(lhs).to.be.oneOf(rhs);
   332	            break;
   333	          case 'notIn':
   334	            expect(lhs).to.not.be.oneOf(rhs);
   335	            break;
   336	          case 'contains':
   337	            expect(lhs).to.include(rhs);
   338	            break;
   339	          case 'notContains':
   340	            expect(lhs).to.not.include(rhs);
   341	            break;
   342	          case 'length':
   343	            expect(lhs).to.have.lengthOf(rhs);
   344	            break;
   345	          case 'matches':
   346	            expect(lhs).to.match(new RegExp(rhs));
   347	            break;
   348	          case 'notMatches':
   349	            expect(lhs).to.not.match(new RegExp(rhs));
   350	            break;
   351	          case 'startsWith':
   352	            expect(lhs).to.startWith(rhs);
   353	            break;
   354	          case 'endsWith':
   355	            expect(lhs).to.endWith(rhs);
   356	            break;
   357	          case 'between':
   358	            const [min, max] = rhs;
   359	            expect(lhs).to.be.within(min, max);
   360	            break;
   361	          case 'isEmpty':
   362	            expect(lhs).to.be.empty;
   363	            break;
   364	          case 'isNotEmpty':
   365	            expect(lhs).to.not.be.empty;
   366	            break;
   367	          case 'isNull':
   368	            expect(lhs).to.be.null;
   369	            break;
   370	          case 'isUndefined':
   371	            expect(lhs).to.be.undefined;
   372	            break;
   373	          case 'isDefined':
   374	            expect(lhs).to.not.be.undefined;
   375	            break;
   376	          case 'isTruthy':
   377	            expect(lhs).to.be.true;
   378	            break;
   379	          case 'isFalsy':
   380	            expect(lhs).to.be.false;
   381	            break;
   382	          case 'isJson':
   383	            expect(lhs).to.be.json;
   384	            break;
   385	          case 'isNumber':
   386	            expect(lhs).to.be.a('number');
   387	            break;
   388	          case 'isString':
   389	            expect(lhs).to.be.a('string');
   390	            break;
   391	          case 'isBoolean':
   392	            expect(lhs).to.be.a('boolean');
   393	            break;
   394	          case 'isArray':
   395	            expect(lhs).to.be.a('array');
   396	            break;
   397	          default:
   398	            expect(lhs).to.equal(rhs);
   399	            break;
   400	        }
   401	
   402	        assertionResults.push({
   403	          uid: nanoid(),
   404	          lhsExpr,
   405	          rhsExpr,
   406	          rhsOperand,
   407	          operator,
   408	          status: 'pass'
   409	        });
   410	      } catch (err) {
   411	        assertionResults.push({
   412	          uid: nanoid(),
   413	          lhsExpr,
   414	          rhsExpr,
   415	          rhsOperand,
   416	          operator,
   417	          status: 'fail',
   418	          error: err.message
   419	        });
   420	      }
   421	    }
   422	
   423	    request.assertionResults = assertionResults;
   424	
   425	    return assertionResults;
   426	  }
   427	}
   428	
   429	module.exports = AssertRuntime;
   430

  describe('bru.setVar random variable', () => {
    it('should be able to set random variables as values', async () => {
      const script = `bru.setVar('title', '{{$randomFirstName}}')`;

      const runtime = new ScriptRuntime({ runtime: 'nodevm' });

      const result = await runtime.runRequestScript(script, {}, {}, {}, '.', null, process.env);

      expect(result.runtimeVariables.title).toBe('{{$randomFirstName}}');
    });
  });

  describe('assert-runtime', () => {
    const baseRequest = {
      method: 'GET',
      url: 'http://localhost:3000/',
      headers: {},
      data: undefined
    };

    const makeResponse = (data) => ({
      status: 200,
      statusText: 'OK',
      data,
      headers: {}
    });

    const runAssertions = (assertions, response, runtime = 'nodevm') => {
      const assertRuntime = new AssertRuntime({ runtime });
      return assertRuntime.runAssertions(assertions, { ...baseRequest }, response, {}, {}, process.env);
    };

    describe('isJson', () => {
      it('should pass for a plain object', () => {
        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          makeResponse({ id: 1, name: 'test' })
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('pass');
      });

      it('should pass for a nested object', () => {
        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          makeResponse({ user: { id: 1, tags: ['a', 'b'] } })
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('pass');
      });

      it('should pass for objects from a different realm (e.g. after res.setBody in node-vm)', async () => {
        const response = makeResponse({ id: 1, name: 'original' });

        // res.setBody() inside node-vm creates a cross-realm object whose
        // constructor is the VM's Object, not the host's Object
        const scriptRuntime = new ScriptRuntime({ runtime: 'nodevm' });
        await scriptRuntime.runResponseScript(
          `res.setBody({ id: 2, name: 'updated' });`,
          { ...baseRequest },
          response,
          {}, {}, '.', null, process.env
        );

        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          response
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('pass');
      });

      it('should fail for an array', () => {
        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          makeResponse([1, 2, 3])
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('fail');
      });

      it('should fail for a string', () => {
        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          makeResponse('hello')
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('fail');
      });

      it('should fail for null', () => {
        const results = runAssertions(
          [{ name: 'res.body', value: 'isJson', enabled: true }],
          makeResponse(null)
        );
        expect(results[0].status).toBe('fail');
      });
    });
  });

      const { data: requestData, dataBuffer: requestDataBuffer } = parseDataFromRequest(request);

      // Remove false Content-Type header (used to stop axios from auto-setting it); no Content-Type was actually set or sent.
      const headersSent = { ...request.headers };
      Object.keys(headersSent).forEach((key) => {
        if (key.toLowerCase() === 'content-type' && headersSent[key] === false) {
          delete headersSent[key];
        }
      });

      let requestSent = {
        url: request.url,
        method: request.method,
        headers: headersSent,
        data: requestData,
        dataBuffer: requestDataBuffer,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      };

      !runInBackground && mainWindow.webContents.send('main:run-request-event', {
        type: 'request-sent',
        requestSent,
        collectionUid,
        itemUid: item.uid,
        requestUid,
        cancelTokenUid
      });

      if (request.oauth2Credentials?.credentials && request.oauth2Credentials?.credentialsId) {
        mainWindow.webContents.send('main:credentials-update', {
          credentials: request?.oauth2Credentials?.credentials,
          url: request?.oauth2Credentials?.url,
          collectionUid,
          credentialsId: request?.oauth2Credentials?.credentialsId,
          ...(request?.oauth2Credentials?.folderUid ? { folderUid: request.oauth2Credentials.folderUid } : { itemUid: item.uid }),
          debugInfo: request?.oauth2Credentials?.debugInfo
        });

        const { credentialsId, credentials } = request.oauth2Credentials;
        request.oauth2CredentialVariables = request.oauth2CredentialVariables || {};
        Object.entries(credentials).forEach(([key, value]) => {
          request.oauth2CredentialVariables[`$oauth2.${credentialsId}.${key}`] = value;
        });
      }

      let response, responseTime, axiosDataStream;
      try {
        /** @type {import('axios').AxiosResponse} */
        response = await axiosInstance(request);
        isResponseStream = hasStreamHeaders(response.headers);

        if (!isResponseStream) {
          response.data = await promisifyStream(response.data);
        }

        // Prevents the duration on leaking to the actual result
        responseTime = response.headers.get('request-duration');
        response.headers.delete('request-duration');
      } catch (error) {
        deleteCancelToken(cancelTokenUid);

        // if it's a cancel request, don't continue
        if (axios.isCancel(error)) {
          // we are not rejecting the promise here and instead returning a response object with `error` which is handled in the `send-http-request` invocation
          // timeline prop won't be accessible in the usual way in the renderer process if we reject the promise
          return {
            statusText: 'REQUEST_CANCELLED',
            isCancel: true,
            error: 'REQUEST_CANCELLED',
            timeline: error.timeline
          };
        }
        if (error?.response) {
          response = error.response;

          // Prevents the duration on leaking to the actual result
          responseTime = response.headers.get('request-duration');
          response.headers.delete('request-duration');
          isResponseStream = hasStreamHeaders(response.headers);
          if (!isResponseStream) {
            response.data = await promisifyStream(response.data);
          }
        } else {
          await executeRequestOnFailHandler(request, error);

          // if it's not a network error, don't continue
          // we are not rejecting the promise here and instead returning a response object with `error` which is handled in the `send-http-request` invocation
          // timeline prop won't be accessible in the usual way in the renderer process if we reject the promise
          return {
            statusText: error.statusText,

    33	  const seen = new WeakSet();
    34	  return (key, value) => {
    35	    if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
    36	      if (seen.has(value)) return '[Circular]';
    37	      seen.add(value);
    38	    }
    39	    return value;

    62	const simpleHash = (str) => {
    63	  let hash = 0;
    64	  for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
    65	    const char = str.charCodeAt(i);
    66	    hash = (hash << 5) - hash + char;
    67	    hash &= hash; // Convert to 32bit integer
    68	  }
    69	  return new Uint32Array([hash])[0].toString(36);
    70	};
    71	
    72	const generateUidBasedOnHash = (str) => {
    73	  const hash = simpleHash(str);
    74	
    75	  return `${hash}`.padEnd(21, '0');
    76	};

    78	const flattenDataForDotNotation = (data) => {
    79	  var result = {};
    80	  function recurse(current, prop) {
    81	    if (Object(current) !== current) {
    82	      result[prop] = current;
    83	    } else if (Array.isArray(current)) {
    84	      for (var i = 0, l = current.length; i < l; i++) {
    85	        recurse(current[i], prop + '[' + i + ']');
    86	      }
    87	      if (l == 0) {
    88	        result[prop] = [];
    89	      }
    90	    } else {
    91	      var isEmpty = true;
    92	      for (var p in current) {
    93	        isEmpty = false;
    94	        recurse(current[p], prop ? prop + '.' + p : p);
    95	      }
    96	      if (isEmpty && prop) {
    97	        result[prop] = {};
    98	      }
    99	    }
   100	  }
   101	
   102	  recurse(data, '');
   103	  return result;
   104	};

   106	const parseDataFromResponse = (response, disableParsingResponseJson = false) => {
   107	  // Parse the charset from content type: https://stackoverflow.com/a/33192813
   108	  const charsetMatch = /charset=([^()<>@,;:"/[\]?.=\s]*)/i.exec(response.headers['content-type'] || '');
   109	  // https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/RegExp/exec#using_exec_with_regexp_literals
   110	  const charsetValue = charsetMatch?.[1];
   111	  const dataBuffer = Buffer.from(response.data);
   112	  // Overwrite the original data for backwards compatibility
   113	  let data;
   114	  if (iconv.encodingExists(charsetValue)) {
   115	    data = iconv.decode(dataBuffer, charsetValue);
   116	  } else {
   117	    data = iconv.decode(dataBuffer, 'utf-8');
   118	  }
   119	  // Try to parse response to JSON, this can quietly fail
   120	  try {
   121	    // Filter out ZWNBSP character
   122	    // https://gist.github.com/antic183/619f42b559b78028d1fe9e7ae8a1352d
   123	    data = data.replace(/^\uFEFF/, '');
   124	    if (!disableParsingResponseJson) {
   125	      data = JSON.parse(data);
   126	    }
   127	  } catch { }
   128	
   129	  return { data, dataBuffer };
   130	};
   131	
   132	const parseDataFromRequest = (request) => {
   133	  let requestDataString;
   134	
   135	  // File uploads are redacted, multipart FormData is formatted from original data for readability, and other types are stringified as-is.
   136	  if (request.mode === 'file') {
   137	    requestDataString = '<request body redacted>';
   138	  } else if (isFormData(request?.data) && Array.isArray(request._originalMultipartData)) {
   139	    const boundary = request.data._boundary || 'boundary';
   140	    requestDataString = formatMultipartData(request._originalMultipartData, boundary);
   141	  } else {
   142	    requestDataString = typeof request?.data === 'string' ? request?.data : safeStringifyJSON(request?.data);
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  const requestCopy = cloneDeep(request);
   146	  if (!requestCopy.data) {
   147	    return { data: null, dataBuffer: null };
   148	  }
   149	  requestCopy.data = requestDataString;
   150	  return parseDataFromResponse(requestCopy);

    22	const toNumber = (value) => {
    23	  const num = Number(value);
    24	  return Number.isInteger(num) ? parseInt(value, 10) : parseFloat(value);
    25	};
    26	
    27	const removeQuotes = (str) => {
    28	  if ((str.startsWith('"') && str.endsWith('"')) || (str.startsWith('\'') && str.endsWith('\''))) {
    29	    return str.slice(1, -1);
    30	  }
    31	  return str;
    32	};
    33	
    34	const executeQuickJsVm = ({ script: externalScript, context: externalContext, scriptType = 'template-literal' }) => {
    35	  if (!externalScript?.length || typeof externalScript !== 'string') {
    36	    return externalScript;
    37	  }
    38	  externalScript = externalScript?.trim();
    39	
    40	  if (scriptType === 'template-literal') {
    41	    if (!isNaN(Number(externalScript))) {
    42	      const number = Number(externalScript);
    43	
    44	      // Check if the number is too high. Too high number might get altered, see #1000
    45	      if (number > Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER) {
    46	        return externalScript;
    47	      }
    48	
    49	      return toNumber(externalScript);
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    if (externalScript === 'true') return true;
    53	    if (externalScript === 'false') return false;
    54	    if (externalScript === 'null') return null;
    55	    if (externalScript === 'undefined') return undefined;
    56	
    57	    externalScript = removeQuotes(externalScript);
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  const vm = QuickJSSyncContext;
    61	
    62	  try {
    63	    const { bru, req, res, ...variables } = externalContext;
    64	
    65	    bru && addBruShimToContext(vm, bru);
    66	    req && addBrunoRequestShimToContext(vm, req);
    67	    res && addBrunoResponseShimToContext(vm, res);
    68	
    69	    Object.entries(variables)?.forEach(([key, value]) => {
    70	      vm.setProp(vm.global, key, marshallToVm(value, vm));
    71	    });
    72	
    73	    const templateLiteralText = `\`${externalScript}\``;
    74	    const jsExpressionText = `${externalScript}`;
    75	
    76	    let scriptText = scriptType === 'template-literal' ? templateLiteralText : jsExpressionText;
    77	
    78	    const result = vm.evalCode(scriptText);
    79	    if (result.error) {
    80	      let e = vm.dump(result.error);
    81	      result.error.dispose();
    82	      return e;
    83	    } else {
    84	      let v = vm.dump(result.value);
    85	      result.value.dispose();
    86	      return v;
    87	    }
    88	  } catch (error) {
    89	    console.error('Error executing the script!', error);
    90	  }
    91	};
